### <a id="the-inductive-types-h-s-p-v">The Inductive Types H, S, P, V</a>

This section presents the [Varieties.Varieties][] module of the [Agda Universal Algebra Library][].

<pre class="Agda">

<a id="329" class="Symbol">{-#</a> <a id="333" class="Keyword">OPTIONS</a> <a id="341" class="Pragma">--without-K</a> <a id="353" class="Pragma">--exact-split</a> <a id="367" class="Pragma">--safe</a> <a id="374" class="Symbol">#-}</a>

<a id="379" class="Keyword">open</a> <a id="384" class="Keyword">import</a> <a id="391" href="Algebras.Signatures.html" class="Module">Algebras.Signatures</a> <a id="411" class="Keyword">using</a> <a id="417" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="418" href="Algebras.Signatures.html#1239" class="Function">Signature</a><a id="427" class="Symbol">;</a> <a id="429" href="Overture.Preliminaries.html#6863" class="Generalizable">𝓞</a><a id="430" class="Symbol">;</a> <a id="432" href="Universes.html#262" class="Generalizable">𝓥</a><a id="433" class="Symbol">)</a>
<a id="435" class="Keyword">open</a> <a id="440" class="Keyword">import</a> <a id="447" href="MGS-Subsingleton-Theorems.html" class="Module">MGS-Subsingleton-Theorems</a> <a id="473" class="Keyword">using</a> <a id="479" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="480" href="MGS-Subsingleton-Theorems.html#3468" class="Function">global-dfunext</a><a id="494" class="Symbol">)</a>

<a id="497" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="504" href="Varieties.Varieties.html" class="Module">Varieties.Varieties</a> <a id="524" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="525" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#525" class="Bound">𝑆</a> <a id="527" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="529" href="Algebras.Signatures.html#1239" class="Function">Signature</a> <a id="539" href="Overture.Preliminaries.html#6863" class="Generalizable">𝓞</a> <a id="541" href="Universes.html#262" class="Generalizable">𝓥</a><a id="542" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="544" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#544" class="Bound">gfe</a> <a id="548" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="550" href="MGS-Subsingleton-Theorems.html#3468" class="Function">global-dfunext</a><a id="564" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="566" class="Keyword">where</a>

<a id="573" class="Keyword">open</a> <a id="578" class="Keyword">import</a> <a id="585" href="Varieties.EquationalLogic.html" class="Module">Varieties.EquationalLogic</a> <a id="611" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="612" class="Argument">𝑆</a> <a id="614" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="616" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#525" class="Bound">𝑆</a><a id="617" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="619" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#544" class="Bound">gfe</a><a id="622" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="624" class="Keyword">public</a>

</pre>


Fix a signature 𝑆, let 𝒦 be a class of 𝑆-algebras, and define

* H 𝒦 = algebras isomorphic to a homomorphic image of a members of 𝒦;
* S 𝒦 = algebras isomorphic to a subalgebra of a member of 𝒦;
* P 𝒦 = algebras isomorphic to a product of members of 𝒦.

A straight-forward verification confirms that H, S, and P are **closure operators** (expansive, monotone, and idempotent).  A class 𝒦 of 𝑆-algebras is said to be *closed under the taking of homomorphic images* provided `H 𝒦 ⊆ 𝒦`. Similarly, 𝒦 is *closed under the taking of subalgebras* (resp., *arbitrary products*) provided `S 𝒦 ⊆ 𝒦` (resp., `P 𝒦 ⊆ 𝒦`). The operators H, S, and P can be composed with one another repeatedly, forming yet more closure operators.

An algebra is a homomorphic image (resp., subalgebra; resp., product) of every algebra to which it is isomorphic. Thus, the class `H 𝒦` (resp., `S 𝒦`; resp., `P 𝒦`) is closed under isomorphism.

A **variety** is a class of algebras, in the same signature, that is closed under the taking of homomorphic images, subalgebras, and arbitrary products.  To represent varieties we define inductive types for the closure operators `H`, `S`, and `P` that are composable.  Separately, we define an inductive type `V` which simultaneously represents closure under all three operators, `H`, `S`, and `P`.




#### <a id="homomorphic-closure">Homomorphic closure</a>

We define the inductive type `H` to represent classes of algebras that include all homomorphic images of algebras in the class; i.e., classes that are closed under the taking of homomorphic images.

<pre class="Agda">

#### <a id="subalgebraic-closure">Subalgebraic closure</a>

The most useful inductive type that we have found for representing the semantic notion of a class of algebras that is closed under the taking of subalgebras is the following.

<pre class="Agda">

</pre>



#### <a id="product-closure">Product closure</a>

The most useful inductive type that we have found for representing the semantic notion of an class of algebras closed under the taking of arbitrary products is the following.

<pre class="Agda">

<a id="3559" class="Keyword">data</a> <a id="P"></a><a id="3564" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#3564" class="Datatype">P</a> <a id="3566" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="3567" <a id="4059" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#525" class="Bound">𝑆</a><a id="4060" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="4062" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="4064" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#4028" class="Bound">𝑨</a> <a id="4066" href="Relations.Discrete.html#2494" class="Function Operator">∈</a> <a id="4068" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#3564" class="Datatype">P</a><a id="4069" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="4070" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#3567" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="4071" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="4073" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#3567" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="4074" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="4076" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#3583" class="Bound">𝒦</a> <a id="4078" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="4080" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#4028" class="Bound">𝑨</a> <a id="4082" href="Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#1049" class="Function Operator">≅</a> <a id="4084" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#4045" class="Bound">𝑩</a> <a id="4086" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="4088" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#4045" class="Bound">𝑩</a> <a id="4090" href="Relations.Discrete.html#2494" class="Function Operator">∈</a> <a id="4092" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#3564" class="Datatype">P</a> <a id="4094" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#3583" class="Bound">𝒦</a>
 <a id="P.pisow"></a><a id="4097" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#4097" class="InductiveConstructor">pisow</a>  <a id="4104" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="4106" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="4107" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#4107" class="Bound">𝑨</a> <a id="4109" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#4109" class="Bound">𝑩</a> <a id="4111" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="4113" href="Algebras.Algebras.html#674" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="4121" class="Symbol">_</a> <a id="4123" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#525" class="Bound">𝑆</a><a id="4124" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="4126" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="4128" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#4107" class="Bound">𝑨</a> <a id="4130" href="Relations.Discrete.html#2494" class="Function Operator">∈</a> <a id="4132" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#3564" class="Datatype">P</a><a id="4133" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="4134" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#3567" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="4135" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="4137" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#3569" class="Bound">𝓦</a><a id="4138" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="4140" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#3583" class="Bound">𝒦</a> <a id="4142" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="4144" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#4107" class="Bound">𝑨</a> <a id="4146" href="Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#1049" class="Function Operator">≅</a> <a id="4148" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#4109" class="Bound">𝑩</a> <a id="4150" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="4152" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#4109" class="Bound">𝑩</a> <a id="4154" href="Relations.Discrete.html#2494" class="Function Operator">∈</a> <a id="4156" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#3564" class="Datatype">P</a> <a id="4158" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#3583" class="Bound">𝒦</a>

</pre>



#### <a id="varietal-closure">Varietal closure</a>

A class 𝒦 of 𝑆-algebras is called a **variety** if it is closed under each of the closure operators H, S, and P introduced above; the corresponding closure operator is often denoted 𝕍, but we will denote it by `V`.

We now define `V` as an inductive type.

<pre class="Agda">

<a id="4498" class="Keyword">data</a> <a id="V"></a><a id="4503" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#4503" class="Datatype">V</a> <a id="4505" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="4506" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#4506" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="4508" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#4508" class="Bound">𝓦</a> <a id="4510" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="4512" href="Agda.Primitive.html#423" class="Function">Universe</a><a id="4520" class="Symbol">}(</a><a id="4522" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#4522" class="Bound">𝒦</a> <a id="4524" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="4526" href="Relations.Discrete.html#1638" class="Function">Pred</a><a id="4530" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="4531" href="Algebras.Algebras.html#674" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="4539" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#4506" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="4541" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#525" class="Bound">𝑆</a><a id="4542" class="Symbol">)(</a><a id="4544" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="4566" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#4506" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="4568" href="Agda.Primitive.html#636" class="Function Operator">⊔</a> <a id="4570" id="5151" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#4508" class="Bound">𝓦</a><a id="5152" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="5154" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#4522" class="Bound">𝒦</a><a id="5155" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="5157" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="5159" href="Algebras.Products.html#1173" class="Function">⨅</a> <a id="5161" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#5108" class="Bound">𝒜</a> <a id="5163" href="Relations.Discrete.html#2494" class="Function Operator">∈</a> <a id="5165" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#4503" class="Datatype">V</a> <a id="5167" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#4522" class="Bound">𝒦</a>
 <a id="V.visou"></a><a id="5170" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#5170" class="InductiveConstructor">visou</a>  <a id="5177" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="5179" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="5180" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#5180" class="Bound">𝑨</a> <a id="5182" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="5184" href="Algebras.Algebras.html#674" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="5192" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#4506" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="5194" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#525" class="Bound">𝑆</a><a id="5195" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="5197" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#5197" class="Bound">𝑩</a> <a id="5199" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="5201" href="Algebras.Algebras.html#674" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="5209" class="Symbol">_</a> <a id="5211" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#525" class="Bound">𝑆</a><a id="5212" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="5214" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="5216" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#5180" class="Bound">𝑨</a> <a id="5218" href="Relations.Discrete.html#2494" class="Function Operator">∈</a> <a id="5220" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#4503" class="Datatype">V</a><a id="5221" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="5222" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#4506" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="5223" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="5225" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#4506" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="5226" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="5228" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#4522" class="Bound">𝒦</a> <a id="5230" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="5232" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#5180" class="Bound">𝑨</a> <a id="5234" href="Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#1049" class="Function Operator">≅</a> <a id="5236" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#5197" class="Bound">𝑩</a> <a id="5238" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="5240" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#5197" class="Bound">𝑩</a> <a id="5242" href="Relations.Discrete.html#2494" class="Function Operator">∈</a> <a id="5244" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#4503" class="Datatype">V</a> <a id="5246" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#4522" class="Bound">𝒦</a>
 <a id="V.visow"></a><a id="5249" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#5249" class="InductiveConstructor">visow</a>  <a id="5256" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="5258" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="5259" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#5259" class="Bound">𝑨</a> <a id="5261" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#5261" class="Bound">𝑩</a> <a id="5263" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="5265" href="Algebras.Algebras.html#674" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="5273" class="Symbol">_</a> <a id="5275" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#525" class="Bound">𝑆</a><a id="5276" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="5278" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="5280" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#5259" class="Bound">𝑨</a> <a id="5282" href="Relations.Discrete.html#2494" class="Function Operator">∈</a> <a id="5284" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#4503" class="Datatype">V</a><a id="5285" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="5286" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#4506" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="5287" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="5289" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#4508" class="Bound">𝓦</a><a id="5290" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="5292" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#4522" class="Bound">𝒦</a> <a id="5294" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="5296" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#5259" class="Bound">𝑨</a> <a id="5298" href="Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#1049" class="Function Operator">≅</a> <a id="5300" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#5261" class="Bound">𝑩</a> <a id="5302" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="5304" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#5261" class="Bound">𝑩</a> <a id="5306" href="Relations.Discrete.html#2494" class="Function Operator">∈</a> <a id="5308" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#4503" class="Datatype">V</a> <a id="5310" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#4522" class="Bound">𝒦</a>

</pre>

Thus, if 𝒦 is a class of 𝑆-algebras, then the **variety generated by** 𝒦 is denoted by `V 𝒦` and defined to be the smallest class that contains 𝒦 and is closed under `H`, `S`, and `P`.

With the closure operator V representing closure under HSP, we represent formally what it means to be a variety of algebras as follows.

<pre class="Agda">

<a id="is-variety"></a><a id="5662" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#5662" class="Function">is-variety</a> <a id="5673" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="5675" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="5676" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#5676" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="5678" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="5680" href="Agda.Primitive.html#423" class="Function">Universe</a><a id="5688" class="Symbol">}(</a><a id="5690" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#5690" class="Bound">𝒱</a> <a id="5692" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="5694" href="Relations.Discrete.html#1638" class="Function">Pred</a> <a id="5699" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="5700" href="Algebras.Algebras.html#674" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="5708" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#5676" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="5710" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#525" class="Bound">𝑆</a><a id="5711" class="Symbol">)(</a><a id="5713" href="Algebras.Products.html#2276" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="5716" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#5676" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="5717" class="Symbol">))</a> <a id="5720" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="5722" href="Algebras.Products.html#2276" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="5725" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#5676" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="5727" href="Universes.html#403" class="Function Operator">̇</a>
<a id="5729" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#5662" class="Function">is-variety</a><a id="5739" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="5740" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#5740" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="5741" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="5743" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#5743" class="Bound">𝒱</a> <a id="5745" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="5747" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#4503" class="Datatype">V</a><a id="5748" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="5749" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#5740" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="5750" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="5752" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#5740" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="5753" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="5755" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#5743" class="Bound">𝒱</a> <a id="5757" href="Relations.Discrete.html#2760" class="Function Operator">⊆</a> <a id="5759" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#5743" class="Bound">𝒱</a>

<a id="variety"></a><a id="5762" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#5762" class="Function">variety</a> <a id="5770" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="5772" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="5773" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#5773" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="5775" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="5777" href="Agda.Primitive.html#423" class="Function">Universe</a><a id="5785" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="5787" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="5789" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="5790" href="Algebras.Products.html#2276" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="5793" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#5773" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="5794" class="Symbol">)</a><a id="5795" href="Agda.Primitive.html#606" class="Function Operator">⁺</a> <a id="5797" href="Universes.html#403" class="Function Operator">̇</a>
<a id="5799" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#5762" class="Function">variety</a> <a id="5807" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#5807" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="5809" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="5811" href="MGS-MLTT.html#3074" class="Function">Σ</a> <a id="5813" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#5813" class="Bound">𝒱</a> <a id="5815" href="MGS-MLTT.html#3074" class="Function">꞉</a> <a id="5817" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="5818" href="Relations.Discrete.html#1638" class="Function">Pred</a> <a id="5823" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="5824" href="Algebras.Algebras.html#674" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="5832" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#5807" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="5834" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#525" class="Bound">𝑆</a><a id="5835" class="Symbol">)(</a><a id="5837" href="Algebras.Products.html#2276" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="5840" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#5807" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="5841" class="Symbol">))</a> <a id="5844" href="MGS-MLTT.html#3074" class="Function">,</a> <a id="5846" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#5662" class="Function">is-variety</a> <a id="5857" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#5813" class="Bound">𝒱</a>

</pre>


#### <a id="V-is-closed-under-lift">V is closed under lift</a>

As mentioned earlier, a technical hurdle that must be overcome when formalizing proofs in Agda is the proper handling of universe levels. In particular, in the proof of the Birkhoff's theorem, for example, we will need to know that if an algebra 𝑨 belongs to the variety V 𝒦, then so does the lift of 𝑨.  Let us get the tedious proof of this technical lemma out of the way.

<pre class="Agda">

<a id="6326" class="Keyword">open</a> <a id="6331" href="Overture.Lifts.html#2588" class="Module">Lift</a>
<a id="6336" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="6343" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#6343" class="Module">_</a> <a id="6345" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="6346" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#6346" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="6348" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="6350" href="Agda.Primitive.html#423" class="Function">Universe</a><a id="6358" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="6360" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#6360" class="Bound">𝒦</a> <a id="6362" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="6364" href="Relations.Discrete.html#1638" class="Function">Pred</a> <a id="6369" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="6370" href="Algebras.Algebras.html#674" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="6378" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#6346" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="6380" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#525" class="Bound">𝑆</a><a id="6381" class="Symbol">)(</a><a id="6383" href="Algebras.Products.html#2276" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="6386" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#6346" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="6387" class="Symbol">)}</a> <a id="6390" class="Keyword">where</a>

 <a id="6398" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#6398" class="Function">VlA</a> <a id="6402" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="6404" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="6405" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#6405" class="Bound">𝑨</a> <a id="6407" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="6409" href="Algebras.Algebras.html#674" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="6417" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="6418" href="Algebras.Products.html#2276" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="6421" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#6346" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="6422" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="6424" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#525" class="Bound">𝑆</a><a id="6425" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="6427" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="6429" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#6405" class="Bound">𝑨</a> <a id="6431" href="Relations.Discrete.html#2494" class="Function Operator">∈</a> <a id="6433" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#4503" class="Datatype">V</a><a id="6434" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="6435" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#6346" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="6436" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="6438" href="Algebras.Products.html#2276" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="6441" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#6346" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="6442" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="6444" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#6360" class="Bound">𝒦</a>
       <a id="6453" class="Comment">------------------------------------------</a>
  <a id="6498" class="Symbol">→</a>    <a id="6503" href="Algebras.Algebras.html#4650" class="Function">lift-alg</a> <a id="6512" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#6405" class="Bound">𝑨</a> <a id="6514" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="6515" href="Algebras.Products.html#2276" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="6518" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#6346" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="6520" href="Agda.Primitive.html#606" class="Function Operator">⁺</a><a id="6521" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="6523" href="Relations.Discrete.html#2494" class="Function Operator">∈</a> <a id="6525" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#4503" class="Datatype">V</a><a id="6526" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="6527" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#6346" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="6528" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="6530" href="Algebras.Products.html#2276" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="6533" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#6346" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="6535" href="Agda.Primitive.html#606" class="Function Operator">⁺</a><a id="6536" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="6538" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#6360" class="Bound">𝒦</a>

 <a id="7707" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#6398" class="Function">VlA</a> <a id="7711" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="7712" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#5170" class="InductiveConstructor">visou</a><a id="7717" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="7718" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#7718" class="Bound">𝑨</a><a id="7719" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="7721" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#7721" class="Bound">𝑩</a><a id="7722" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="7724" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#7724" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="7726" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#7726" class="Bound">A≅B</a><a id="7729" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="7731" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="7733" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#5249" class="InductiveConstructor">visow</a> <a id="7739" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="7740" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#4651" class="InductiveConstructor">vlift</a> <a id="7746" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#7724" class="Bound">x</a><a id="7747" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="7749" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="7750" href="Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#3489" class="Function">lift-alg-iso</a> <a id="7763" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#7726" class="Bound">A≅B</a><a id="7766" class="Symbol">)</a>
 <a id="7769" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#6398" class="Function">VlA</a> <a id="7773" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="7774" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#5249" class="InductiveConstructor">visow</a><a id="7779" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="7780" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#7780" class="Bound">𝑨</a><a id="7781" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="7783" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#7783" class="Bound">𝑩</a><a id="7784" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="7786" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#7786" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="7788" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#7788" class="Bound">A≅B</a><a id="7791" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="7793" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="7795" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#5249" class="InductiveConstructor">visow</a> <a id="7801" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="7802" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#6398" class="Function">VlA</a> <a id="7806" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#7786" class="Bound">x</a><a id="7807" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="7809" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="7810" href="Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#3489" class="Function">lift-alg-iso</a> <a id="7823" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#7788" class="Bound">A≅B</a><a id="7826" class="Symbol">)</a>

</pre>



#### <a id="closure-properties">Closure properties</a>

The types defined above represent operators with useful closure properties. We now prove a handful of such properties that we need later.

First, `P` is a closure operator.  This is proved by checking that `P` is *monotone*, *expansive*, and *idempotent*. The meaning of these terms will be clear from the definitions of the types that follow.

<pre class="Agda">

 <a id="9003" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#8901" class="Function">P-idemp</a> <a id="9011" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="9012" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#3655" class="InductiveConstructor">pbase</a> <a id="9018" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#9018" class="Bound">x</a><a id="9019" class="Symbol">)</a>    <a id="9024" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="9026" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#3777" class="InductiveConstructor">pliftw</a> <a id="9033" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#9018" class="Bound">x</a>

 <a id="9174" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#8901" class="Function">P-idemp</a> <a id="9182" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="9183" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#3936" class="InductiveConstructor">prodw</a> <a id="9189" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#9189" class="Bound">x</a><a id="9190" class="Symbol">)</a>    <a id="9195" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="9197" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#3936" class="InductiveConstructor">prodw</a> <a id="9203" class="Symbol">(λ</a> <a id="9206" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#9206" class="Bound">i</a> <a id="9208" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="9210" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#8901" class="Function">P-idemp</a> <a id="9218" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="9219" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#9189" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="9221" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#9206" class="Bound">i</a><a id="9222" class="Symbol">))</a>

 <a id="9271" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#8901" class="Function">P-idemp</a> <a id="9279" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="9280" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#4097" class="InductiveConstructor">pisow</a> <a id="9286" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#9286" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="9288" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#9288" class="Bound">x₁</a><a id="9290" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="9292" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="9294" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#4097" class="InductiveConstructor">pisow</a> <a id="9300" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="9301" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#8901" class="Function">P-idemp</a> <a id="9309" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#9286" class="Bound">x</a><a id="9310" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="9312" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#9288" class="Bound">x₁</a>

</pre>

Similarly, S is a closure operator.  The facts that S is idempotent and expansive won't be needed below, so we omit these, but we will make use of monotonicity of S.  Here is the proof of the latter.

<pre class="Agda">

<a id="S-mono"></a><a id="9543" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#9543" class="Function">S-mono</a> <a id="9550" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="9552" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="9553" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#9553" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="9555" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#9555" class="Bound">𝓦</a> <a id="9557" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="9559" href="Agda.Primitive.html#423" class="Function">Universe</a><a id="9567" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="9569" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#9569" class="Bound">𝒦</a> <a id="9571" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#9571" class="Bound">𝒦&#39;</a> <a id="9574" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="9576" href="Relations.Discrete.html#1638" class="Function">Pred</a> <a id="9581" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="9582" href="Algebras.Algebras.html#674" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="9590" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#9553" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="9592" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#525" class="Bound">𝑆</a><a id="9593" class="Symbol">)(</a><a id="9595" href="Algebras.Products.html#2276" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="9598" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#9553" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="9599" class="Symbol">)}</a>
 <a id="9603" class="Symbol">→</a>       <a id="9611" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#9569" class="Bound">𝒦</a> <a id="9613" href="Relations.Discrete.html#2760" class="Function Operator">⊆</a> <a id="9615" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#9571" class="Bound">𝒦&#39;</a> <a id="9618" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="9620" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#2875" class="Datatype">S</a><a id="9621" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="9622" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#9553" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="9623" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="9625" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#9555" class="Bound">𝓦</a><a id="9626" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="9628" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#9569" class="Bound">𝒦</a> <a id="9630" href="Relations.Discrete.html#2760" class="Function Operator">⊆</a> <a id="9632" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#2875" class="Datatype">S</a><a id="9633" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="9634" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#9553" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="9635" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="9637" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#9555" class="Bound">𝓦</a><a id="9638" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="9640" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#9571" class="Bound">𝒦&#39;</a>

<a id="9644" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#9543" class="Function">S-mono</a> <a id="9651" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#9651" class="Bound">kk&#39;</a> <a id="9655" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="9656" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#2966" class="InductiveConstructor">sbase</a> <a id="9662" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#9662" class="Bound">x</a><a id="9663" class="Symbol">)</a>            <a id="9676" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="9678" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#2966" class="InductiveConstructor">sbase</a> <a id="9684" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="9685" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#9651" class="Bound">kk&#39;</a> <a id="9689" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#9662" class="Bound">x</a><a id="9690" class="Symbol">)</a>
<a id="9692" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#9543" class="Function">S-mono</a> <a id="9699" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#9699" class="Bound">kk&#39;</a> <a id="9703" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="9704" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#3022" class="InductiveConstructor">slift</a><a id="9709" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="9710" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#9710" class="Bound">𝑨</a><a id="9711" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="9713" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#9713" class="Bound">x</a><a id="9714" class="Symbol">)</a>         <a id="9724" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="9726" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#3022" class="InductiveConstructor">slift</a> <a id="9732" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="9733" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#9543" class="Function">S-mono</a> <a id="9740" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#9699" class="Bound">kk&#39;</a> <a id="9744" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#9713" class="Bound">x</a><a id="9745" class="Symbol">)</a>
<a id="9747" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#9543" class="Function">S-mono</a> <a id="9754" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#9754" class="Bound">kk&#39;</a> <a id="9758" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="9759" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#3086" class="InductiveConstructor">ssub</a><a id="9763" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="9764" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#9764" class="Bound">𝑨</a><a id="9765" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="9767" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#9767" class="Bound">𝑩</a><a id="9768" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="9770" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#9770" class="Bound">sA</a> <a id="9773" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#9773" class="Bound">B≤A</a><a id="9776" class="Symbol">)</a>  <a id="9779" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="9781" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#3086" class="InductiveConstructor">ssub</a> <a id="9786" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="9787" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#9543" class="Function">S-mono</a> <a id="9794" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#9754" class="Bound">kk&#39;</a> <a id="9798" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#9770" class="Bound">sA</a><a id="9800" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="9802" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#9773" class="Bound">B≤A</a>
<a id="9806" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#9543" class="Function">S-mono</a> <a id="9813" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#9813" class="Bound">kk&#39;</a> <a id="9817" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="9818" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#3164" class="InductiveConstructor">ssubw</a><a id="9823" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="9824" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#9824" class="Bound">𝑨</a><a id="9825" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="9827" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#9827" class="Bound">𝑩</a><a id="9828" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="9830" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#9830" class="Bound">sA</a> <a id="9833" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#9833" class="Bound">B≤A</a><a id="9836" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="9838" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="9840" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#3164" class="InductiveConstructor">ssubw</a> <a id="9846" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="9847" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#9543" class="Function">S-mono</a> <a id="9854" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#9813" class="Bound">kk&#39;</a> <a id="9858" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#9830" class="Bound">sA</a><a id="9860" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="9862" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#9833" class="Bound">B≤A</a>
<a id="9866" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#9543" class="Function">S-mono</a> <a id="9873" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#9873" class="Bound">kk&#39;</a> <a id="9877" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="9878" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#3227" class="InductiveConstructor">siso</a> <a id="9883" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#9883" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="9885" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#9885" class="Bound">x₁</a><a id="9887" class="Symbol">)</a>          <a id="9898" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="9900" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#3227" class="InductiveConstructor">siso</a> <a id="9905" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="9906" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#9543" class="Function">S-mono</a> <a id="9913" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#9873" class="Bound">kk&#39;</a> <a id="9917" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#9883" class="Bound">x</a><a id="9918" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="9920" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#9885" class="Bound">x₁</a>

</pre>

We sometimes want to go back and forth between our two representations of subalgebras of algebras in a class. The tools `subalgebra→S` and `S→subalgebra` are made for that purpose.

<pre class="Agda">

<a id="10132" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="10139" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#10139" class="Module">_</a> <a id="10141" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="10142" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#10142" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="10144" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#10144" class="Bound">𝓦</a> <a id="10146" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="10148" href="Agda.Primitive.html#423" class="Function">Universe</a><a id="10156" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="10158" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#10158" class="Bound">𝒦</a> <a id="10160" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="10162" href="Relations.Discrete.html#1638" class="Function">Pred</a> <a id="10167" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="10168" href="Algebras.Algebras.html#674" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="10176" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#10142" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="10178" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#525" class="Bound">𝑆</a><a id="10179" class="Symbol">)(</a><a id="10181" href="Algebras.Products.html#2276" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="10184" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#10142" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="10185" class="Symbol">)}</a> <a id="10188" class="Keyword">where</a>

 <a id="10196" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#10196" class="Function">subalgebra→S</a> <a id="10209" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="10211" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="10212" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#10212" class="Bound">𝑩</a> <a id="10214" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="10216" href="Algebras.Algebras.html#674" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="10224" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="10225" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#10142" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="10227" href="Agda.Primitive.html#636" class="Function Operator">⊔</a> <a id="10229" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#10144" class="Bound">𝓦</a><a id="10230" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="10232" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#525" class="Bound">𝑆</a><a id="10233" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="10235" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="10237" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#10212" class="Bound">𝑩</a> <a id="10239" href="Subalgebras.Subalgebras.html#5248" class="Function Operator">IsSubalgebraOfClass</a> <a id="10259" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#10158" class="Bound">𝒦</a> <a id="10261" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="10263" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#10212" class="Bound">𝑩</a> <a id="10265" href="Relations.Discrete.html#2494" class="Function Operator">∈</a> <a id="10267" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#2875" class="Datatype">S</a><a id="10268" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="10269" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#10142" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="10270" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="10272" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#10144" class="Bound">𝓦</a><a id="10273" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="10275" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#10158" class="Bound">𝒦</a>

 <a id="10279" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#10196" class="Function">subalgebra→S</a> <a id="10292" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="10293" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#10293" class="Bound">𝑩</a><a id="10294" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="10296" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="10297" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#10297" class="Bound">𝑨</a> <a id="10299" href="Overture.Preliminaries.html#11717" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="10301" class="Symbol">((</a><a id="10303" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#10303" class="Bound">𝑪</a> <a id="10305" href="Overture.Preliminaries.html#11717" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="10307" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#10307" class="Bound">C≤A</a><a id="10310" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="10312" href="Overture.Preliminaries.html#11717" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="10314" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#10314" class="Bound">KA</a> <a id="10317" href="Overture.Preliminaries.html#11717" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="10319" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#10319" class="Bound">B≅C</a><a id="10322" class="Symbol">))</a> <a id="10325" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="10327" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#3086" class="InductiveConstructor">ssub</a> <a id="10332" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#10446" class="Function">sA</a> <a id="10335" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#10350" class="Function">B≤A</a>

   <a id="11836" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#11815" class="Function">A≅SA</a> <a id="11841" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="11843" href="Overture.Preliminaries.html#12469" class="Function">snd</a> <a id="11847" href="Overture.Preliminaries.html#12465" class="Function Operator">∥</a> <a id="11849" href="Overture.Preliminaries.html#12469" class="Function">snd</a> <a id="11853" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#11714" class="Function">AS</a> <a id="11856" href="Overture.Preliminaries.html#12465" class="Function Operator">∥</a>

</pre>

Next we observe that lifting to a higher universe does not break the property of being a subalgebra of an algebra of a class.  In other words, if we lift a subalgebra of an algebra in a class, the result is still a subalgebra of an algebra in the class.

<pre class="Agda">
<a id="12139" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="12146" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#12146" class="Module">_</a> <a id="12148" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="12149" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#12149" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="12151" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#12151" class="Bound">𝓦</a> <a id="12153" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="12155" href="Agda.Primitive.html#423" class="Function">Universe</a><a id="12163" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="12165" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#12165" class="Bound">𝒦</a> <a id="12167" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="12169" href="Relations.Discrete.html#1638" class="Function">Pred</a> <a id="12174" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="12175" href="Algebras.Algebras.html#674" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="12183" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#12149" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="12185" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#525" class="Bound">𝑆</a><a id="12186" class="Symbol">)(</a><a id="12188" href="Algebras.Products.html#2276" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="12191" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#12149" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="12192" class="Symbol">)}</a> <a id="12195" class="Keyword">where</a>

  <a id="12239" class="Symbol">→</a>              <a id="12254" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#12220" class="Bound">𝑩</a> <a id="12256" href="Subalgebras.Subalgebras.html#5248" class="Function Operator">IsSubalgebraOfClass</a> <a id="12276" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="12277" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#3564" class="Datatype">P</a><a id="12278" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="12279" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#12149" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="12280" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="12282" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#12149" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="12283" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="12285" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#12165" class="Bound">𝒦</a><a id="12286" class="Symbol">)</a>

 <a id="12421" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#12203" class="Function">lift-alg-subP</a> <a id="12435" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="12436" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#12436" class="Bound">𝑩</a><a id="12437" class="Symbol">}(</a><a id="12439" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#12439" class="Bound">𝑨</a> <a id="12441" href="Overture.Preliminaries.html#11717" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="12443" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="12444" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#12444" class="Bound">𝑪</a> <a id="12446" href="Overture.Preliminaries.html#11717" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="12448" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#12448" class="Bound">C≤A</a><a id="12451" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="12453" href="Overture.Preliminaries.html#11717" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="12455" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#12455" class="Bound">pA</a> <a id="12458" href="Overture.Preliminaries.html#11717" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="12460" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#12460" class="Bound">B≅C</a> <a id="12464" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="12466" class="Symbol">=</a>

The next lemma would be too obvious to care about were it not for the fact that we'll need it later, so it too must be formalized.

We need to formalize one more lemma before arriving the main objective of this section, which is the proof of the inclusion PS⊆SP.

<pre class="Agda">
<a id="14311" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="14318" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#14318" class="Module">_</a> <a id="14320" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="14321" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#14321" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="14323" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#14323" class="Bound">𝓦</a> <a id="14325" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="14327" href="Agda.Primitive.html#423" class="Function">Universe</a><a id="14335" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="14337" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#14337" class="Bound">fe</a> <a id="14340" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="14342" href="MGS-FunExt-from-Univalence.html#2235" class="Function">hfunext</a> <a id="14350" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#14323" class="Bound">𝓦</a> <a id="14352" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#14321" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="14353" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="14355" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#14355" class="Bound">𝒦</a> <a id="14357" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="14359" href="Relations.Discrete.html#1638" class="Function">Pred</a><a id="14363" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="14364" href="Algebras.Algebras.html#674" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="14372" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#14321" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="14374" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#525" class="Bound">𝑆</a><a id="14375" class="Symbol">)(</a><a id="14377" href="Algebras.Products.html#2276" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="14380" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#14321" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="14381" class="Symbol">)}</a> <a id="14384" class="Keyword">where</a>

 <a id="14392" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#14392" class="Function">lemPS⊆SP</a> <a id="14401" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="14403" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="14404" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#14404" class="Bound">I</a> <a id="14406" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="14408" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#14323" class="Bound">𝓦</a> <a id="14410" href="Universes.html#403" class="Function Operator">̇</a><a id="14411" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="14413" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#14413" class="Bound">ℬ</a> <a id="14415" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="14417" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#14404" class="Bound">I</a> <a id="14419" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="14421" href="Algebras.Algebras.html#674" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="14429" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#14321" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="14431" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#525" class="Bound">𝑆</a><a id="14432" class="Symbol">}</a>
  <a id="14436" class="Symbol">→</a>         <a id="14446" class="Symbol">(∀</a> <a id="14449" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#14449" class="Bound">i</a> <a id="14451" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="14453" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="14454" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#14413" class="Bound">ℬ</a> <a id="14456" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#14449" class="Bound">i</a><a id="14457" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="14459" href="Subalgebras.Subalgebras.html#5248" class="Function Operator">IsSubalgebraOfClass</a> <a id="14479" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#14355" class="Bound">𝒦</a><a id="14480" class="Symbol">)</a>
            <a id="14494" class="Comment">-------------------------------------</a>
  <a id="14534" class="Symbol">→</a>         <a id="14544" href="Algebras.Products.html#1173" class="Function">⨅</a> <a id="14546" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#14413" class="Bound">ℬ</a> <a id="14548" href="Subalgebras.Subalgebras.html#5248" class="Function Operator">IsSubalgebraOfClass</a> <a id="14568" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="14569" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#3564" class="Datatype">P</a><a id="14570" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="14571" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#14321" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="14572" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="14574" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#14323" class="Bound">𝓦</a><a id="14575" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="14577" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#14355" class="Bound">𝒦</a><a id="14578" class="Symbol">)</a>

 <a id="14582" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#14392" class="Function">lemPS⊆SP</a> <a id="14591" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="14592" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#14592" class="Bound">I</a><a id="14593" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="14595" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#14595" class="Bound">ℬ</a><a id="14596" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="14598" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#14598" class="Bound">B≤K</a> <a id="14602" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="14604" href="Algebras.Products.html#1173" class="Function">⨅</a> <a id="14606" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#14652" class="Function">𝒜</a> <a id="14608" href="Overture.Preliminaries.html#11717" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="14610" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="14611" href="Algebras.Products.html#1173" class="Function">⨅</a> <a id="14613" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#14697" class="Function">SA</a> <a id="14616" href="Overture.Preliminaries.html#11717" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="14618" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#15172" class="Function">⨅SA≤⨅𝒜</a><a id="14624" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="14626" href="Overture.Preliminaries.html#11717" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="14628" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#15218" class="Function">ξ</a> <a id="14630" href="Overture.Preliminaries.html#11717" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="14632" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="14633" href="Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#4610" class="Function">⨅≅</a> <a id="14636" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#14752" class="Function">B≅SA</a><a id="14640" class="Symbol">)</a>

  <a id="15234" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#15218" class="Function">ξ</a> <a id="15236" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="15238" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#3854" class="InductiveConstructor">produ</a> <a id="15244" class="Symbol">(λ</a> <a id="15247" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#15247" class="Bound">i</a> <a id="15249" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="15251" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#8710" class="Function">P-expa</a> <a id="15258" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="15259" href="Overture.Preliminaries.html#12413" class="Function Operator">∣</a> <a id="15261" href="Overture.Preliminaries.html#12469" class="Function">snd</a> <a id="15265" href="Overture.Preliminaries.html#12465" class="Function Operator">∥</a> <a id="15267" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#14598" class="Bound">B≤K</a> <a id="15271" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#15247" class="Bound">i</a> <a id="15273" href="Overture.Preliminaries.html#12465" class="Function Operator">∥</a> <a id="15275" href="Overture.Preliminaries.html#12413" class="Function Operator">∣</a><a id="15276" class="Symbol">))</a>


</pre>



#### <a id="PS-in-SP">PS(𝒦) ⊆ SP(𝒦)</a>

Finally, we are in a position to prove that a product of subalgebras of algebras in a class 𝒦 is a subalgebra of a product of algebras in 𝒦.

<pre class="Agda">

<a id="15492" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="15499" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#15499" class="Module">_</a> <a id="15501" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="15502" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#15502" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="15504" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="15506" href="Agda.Primitive.html#423" class="Function">Universe</a><a id="15514" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="15516" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#15516" class="Bound">𝒦</a> <a id="15518" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="15520" href="Relations.Discrete.html#1638" class="Function">Pred</a> <a id="15525" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="15526" href="Algebras.Algebras.html#674" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="15534" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#15502" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="15536" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#525" class="Bound">𝑆</a><a id="15537" class="Symbol">)(</a><a id="15539" href="Algebras.Products.html#2276" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="15542" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#15502" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="15543" class="Symbol">)}</a> <a id="15546" class="Keyword">where</a>

 <a id="15554" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#15554" class="Function">PS⊆SP</a> <a id="15560" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="15562" class="Comment">-- extensionality assumption:</a>
            <a id="15604" href="MGS-FunExt-from-Univalence.html#2235" class="Function">hfunext</a> <a id="15612" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="15613" href="Algebras.Products.html#2276" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="15616" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#15502" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="15617" class="Symbol">)(</a><a id="15619" href="Algebras.Products.html#2276" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="15622" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#15502" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="15623" class="Symbol">)</a>

  <a id="15628" class="Symbol">→</a>      <a id="15635" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#3564" class="Datatype">P</a><a id="15636" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="15637" href="Algebras.Products.html#2276" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="15640" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#15502" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="15641" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="15643" href="Algebras.Products.html#2276" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="15646" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#15502" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="15647" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="15649" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="15650"    <a id="16681" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#16619" class="Function">η</a> <a id="16683" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="16685" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#14392" class="Function">lemPS⊆SP</a> <a id="16694" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="16695" href="Algebras.Products.html#2276" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="16698" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#15502" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="16699" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="16701" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="16702" href="Algebras.Products.html#2276" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="16705" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#15502" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="16706" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="16708" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="16709" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#16451" class="Bound">hfe</a><a id="16712" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="16714" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="16715" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#3564" class="Datatype">P</a> <a id="16717" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#15516" class="Bound">𝒦</a><a id="16718" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="16720" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="16721" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#16462" class="Bound">I</a><a id="16722" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="16724" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="16725" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#16465" class="Bound">𝒜</a><a id="16726" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="16728" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#16520" class="Function">ξ</a>

 <a id="16732" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#15554" class="Function">PS⊆SP</a> <a id="16738" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#16738" class="Bound">hfe</a> <a id="16742" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="16743" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#4018" class="InductiveConstructor">pisou</a><a id="16748" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="16749" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#16749" class="Bound">𝑨</a><a id="16750" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="16752" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#16752" class="Bound">𝑩</a><a id="16753" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="16755" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#16755" class="Bound">pA</a> <a id="16758" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#16758" class="Bound">A≅B</a><a id="16761" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="16763" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="16765" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#3227" class="InductiveConstructor">siso</a> <a id="16770" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="16771" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#15554" class="Function">PS⊆SP</a> <a id="16777" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#16738" class="Bound">hfe</a> <a id="16781" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#16755" class="Bound">pA</a><a id="16783" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="16785" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#16758" class="Bound">A≅B</a>
 <a id="16790" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#15554" class="Function">PS⊆SP</a> <a id="16796" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#16796" class="Bound">hfe</a> <a id="16800" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="16801" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#4097" class="InductiveConstructor">pisow</a><a id="16806" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="16807" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#16807" class="Bound">𝑨</a><a id="16808" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="16810" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#16810" class="Bound">𝑩</a><a id="16811" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="16813" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#16813" class="Bound">pA</a> <a id="16816" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#16816" class="Bound">A≅B</a><a id="16819" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="16821" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="16823" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#3227" class="InductiveConstructor">siso</a> <a id="16828" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="16829" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#15554" class="Function">PS⊆SP</a> <a id="16835" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#16796" class="Bound">hfe</a> <a id="16839" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#16813" class="Bound">pA</a><a id="16841" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="16843" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#16816" class="Bound">A≅B</a>

</pre>



#### <a id="more-class-inclusions">More class inclusions</a>

We conclude this subsection with three more inclusion relations that will have bit parts to play later (e.g., in the formal proof of Birkhoff's Theorem).

<a id="17670" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#17435" class="Function">SP⊆V</a> <a id="17675" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="17676" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#3164" class="InductiveConstructor">ssubw</a><a id="17681" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="17682" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#17682" class="Bound">𝑨</a><a id="17683" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="17685" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#17685" class="Bound">𝑩</a><a id="17686" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="17688" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#17688" class="Bound">spA</a> <a id="17692" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#17692" class="Bound">B≤A</a><a id="17695" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="17697" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="17699" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#4944" class="InductiveConstructor">vssubw</a> <a id="17706" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="17707" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#17435" class="Function">SP⊆V</a> <a id="17712" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#17688" class="Bound">spA</a><a id="17715" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="17717" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#17692" class="Bound">B≤A</a>
<a id="17721" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#17435" class="Function">SP⊆V</a> <a id="17726" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="17727" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#3227" class="InductiveConstructor">siso</a> <a id="17732" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#17732" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="17734" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#17734" class="Bound">x₁</a><a id="17736" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="17738" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="17740" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#5249" class="InductiveConstructor">visow</a> <a id="17746" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="17747" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#17435" class="Function">SP⊆V</a> <a id="17752" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#17732" class="Bound">x</a><a id="17753" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="17755" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#17734" class="Bound">x₁</a>

</pre>

We just proved that `SP(𝒦) ⊆ V(𝒦)`, and we did so under fairly general assumptions about the universe level parameters.  Unfortunately, this is sometimes not quite general enough, so we now prove the inclusion again for the specific universe parameters that align with subsequent applications of this result.

<pre class="Agda">

<a id="18095" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="18102" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#18102" class="Module">_</a> <a id="18104" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="18105" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#18105" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="18107" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="18109" href="Agda.Primitive.html#423" class="Function">Universe</a><a id="18117" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="18119" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#18119" class="Bound">𝒦</a> <a id="18121" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="18123" href="Relations.Discrete.html#1638" class="Function">Pred</a> <a id="18128" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="18129" href="Algebras.Algebras.html#674" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="18137" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#18105" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="18139" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#525" class="Bound">𝑆</a><a id="18140" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="18142" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="18143" href="Algebras.Products.html#2276" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="18146" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#18105" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="18147" class="Symbol">)}</a> <a id="18150" class="Keyword">where</a>

 <a id="18158" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#18158" class="Function">SP⊆V&#39;</a> <a id="18164" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="18166" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#2875" class="Datatype">S</a><a id="18167" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="18168" href="Algebras.Products.html#2276" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="18171" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#18105" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="18172" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="18174" href="Algebras.Products.html#2276" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="18177" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#18105" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="18179" href="Agda.Primitive.html#606" class="Function Operator">⁺</a><a id="18180" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="18182" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="18183" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#3564" class="Datatype">P</a><a id="18184" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="18185" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#18105" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="18186" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="18188" href="Algebras.Products.html#2276" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="18191" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#18105" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="18192" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="18194" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#18119" class="Bound">𝒦</a><a id="18195" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="18197" href="Relations.Discrete.html#2760" class="Function Operator">⊆</a> <a id="18199" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#4503" class="Datatype">V</a> <a id="18201" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#18119" class="Bound">𝒦</a>

 <a id="18205" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#18158" class="Function">SP⊆V&#39;</a> <a id="18211" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="18212" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#2966" class="InductiveConstructor">sbase</a><a id="18217" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="18218" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#18218" class="Bound">𝑨</a><a id="18219" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="18221" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#18221" class="Bound">x</a><a id="18222" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="18224" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="18226" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#5249" class="InductiveConstructor">visow</a> <a id="18232" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="18233" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#6398" class="Function">VlA</a> <a id="18237" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="18238" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#17435" class="Function">SP⊆V</a> <a id="18243" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="18244" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#2966" class="InductiveConstructor">sbase</a> <a id="18250" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#18221" class="Bound">x</a><a id="18251" class="Symbol">)))</a> <a id="18255" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="18256" href="Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#1648" class="Function">≅-sym</a> <a id="18262" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="18263" href="Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#4164" class="Function">lift-alg-associative</a> <a id="18284" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#18218" class="Bound">𝑨</a><a id="18285" class="Symbol">))</a>
 <a id="18289" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#18158" class="Function">SP⊆V&#39;</a> <a id="18295" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="18296" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#3022" class="InductiveConstructor">slift</a> <a id="18302" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#18302" class="Bound">x</a><a id="18303" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="18305" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="18307" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#6398" class="Function">VlA</a> <a id="18311" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="18312" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#17435" class="Function">SP⊆V</a> <a id="18317" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#18302" class="Bound">x</a><a id="18318" class="Symbol">)</a>

 <a id="18322" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#18158" class="Function">SP⊆V&#39;</a> <a id="18328" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="18329" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#3086" class="InductiveConstructor">ssub</a><a id="18333" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="18334" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#18334" class="Bound">𝑨</a><a id="18335" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="18337" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#18337" class="Bound">𝑩</a><a id="18338" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="18340" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#18340" class="Bound">spA</a> <a id="18344" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#18344" class="Bound">B≤A</a><a id="18347" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="18349" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="18351" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#4944" class="InductiveConstructor">vssubw</a> <a id="18358" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="18359" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#6398" class="Function">VlA</a> <a id="18363" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="18364" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#17435" class="Function">SP⊆V</a> <a id="18369" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#18340" class="Bound">spA</a><a id="18372" class="Symbol">))</a> <a id="18375" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#18391" class="Function">B≤lA</a>
  <a id="18382" class="Keyword">where</a>
   <a id="18391" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#18391" class="Function">B≤lA</a> <a id="18396" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="18398" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#18337" class="Bound">𝑩</a> <a id="18400" href="Subalgebras.Subalgebras.html#4257" class="Function Operator">≤</a> <a id="18402" href="Algebras.Algebras.html#4650" class="Function">lift-alg</a> <a id="18411" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#18334" class="Bound">𝑨</a> <a id="18413" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="18414" href="Algebras.Products.html#2276" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="18417" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#18105" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="18419" href="Agda.Primitive.html#606" class="Function Operator">⁺</a><a id="18420" class="Symbol">)</a>
   <a id="18425" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#18391" class="Function">B≤lA</a> <a id="18430" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="18432" href="Subalgebras.Subalgebras.html#8660" class="Function">≤-lift-alg</a> <a id="18443" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#18334" class="Bound">𝑨</a> <a id="18445" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#18344" class="Bound">B≤A</a>

 <a id="18451" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#18158" class="Function">SP⊆V&#39;</a> <a id="18457" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="18458" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#3164" class="InductiveConstructor">ssubw</a> <a id="18464" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#18464" class="Bound">spA</a> <a id="18468" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#18468" class="Bound">B≤A</a><a id="18471" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="18473" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="18475" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#4944" class="InductiveConstructor">vssubw</a> <a id="18482" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="18483" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#18158" class="Function">SP⊆V&#39;</a> <a id="18489" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#18464" class="Bound">spA</a><a id="18492" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="18494" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#18468" class="Bound">B≤A</a>

 <a id="18500" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#18158" class="Function">SP⊆V&#39;</a> <a id="18506" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="18507" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#3227" class="InductiveConstructor">siso</a><a id="18511" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="18512" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#18512" class="Bound">𝑨</a><a id="18513" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="18515" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#18515" class="Bound">𝑩</a><a id="18516" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="18518" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#18518" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="18520" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#18520" class="Bound">A≅B</a><a id="18523" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="18525" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="18527" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#5249" class="InductiveConstructor">visow</a> <a id="18533" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="18534" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#6398" class="Function">VlA</a> <a id="18538" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="18539" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#17435" class="Function">SP⊆V</a> <a id="18544" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#18518" class="Bound">x</a><a id="18545" class="Symbol">))</a> <a id="18548" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#18561" class="Function">γ</a>
  <a id="18552" class="Keyword">where</a>
   <a id="18561" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#18561" class="Function">γ</a> <a id="18563" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="18565" href="Algebras.Algebras.html#4650" class="Function">lift-alg</a> <a id="18574" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#18512" class="Bound">𝑨</a> <a id="18576" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="18577" href="Algebras.Products.html#2276" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="18580" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#18105" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="18582" href="Agda.Primitive.html#606" class="Function Operator">⁺</a><a id="18583" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="18585" href="Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#1049" class="Function Operator">≅</a> <a id="18587" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#18515" class="Bound">𝑩</a>
   <a id="18592" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#18561" class="Function">γ</a> <a id="18594" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="18596" href="Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#1826" class="Function">≅-trans</a> <a id="18604" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="18605" href="Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#1648" class="Function">≅-sym</a> <a id="18611" href="Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#2841" class="Function">lift-alg-≅</a><a id="18621" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="18623" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#18520" class="Bound">A≅B</a>

</pre>


#### <a id="S-in-SP">⨅ S(𝒦) ∈ SP(𝒦)</a>

Finally, we prove a result that plays an important role, e.g., in the formal proof of Birkhoff's Theorem. As we saw in [Algebras.Products][], the (informal) product `⨅ S(𝒦)` of all subalgebras of algebras in 𝒦 is implemented (formally) in the [UALib][] as `⨅ 𝔄 S(𝒦)`. Our goal is to prove that this product belongs to `SP(𝒦)`. We do so by first proving that the product belongs to `PS(𝒦)` and then applying the `PS⊆SP` lemma.

Before doing so, we need to redefine the class product so that each factor comes with a map from the type `X` of variable symbols into that factor.  We will explain the reason for this below.

<pre class="Agda">

<a id="19316" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="class-products-with-maps"></a><a id="19323" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#19323" class="Module">class-products-with-maps</a> <a id="19348" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="19349" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#19349" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="19351" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="19353" href="Agda.Primitive.html#423" class="Function">Universe</a><a id="19361" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="19363" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#19363" class="Bound">X</a> <a id="19365" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="19367" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#19349" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="19369" href="Universes.html#403" class="Function Operator">̇</a><a id="19370" class="Symbol">}(</a><a id="19372" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#19372" class="Bound">𝒦</a> <a id="19374" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="19376" href="Relations.Discrete.html#1638" class="Function">Pred</a> <a id="19381" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="19382" href="Algebras.Algebras.html#674" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="19390" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#19349" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="19392" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#525" class="Bound">𝑆</a><a id="19393" class="Symbol">)(</a><a id="19395" href="Algebras.Products.html#2276" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="19398" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#19349" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="19399" class="Symbol">))</a> <a id="19402" class="Keyword">where</a>

 <a id="class-products-with-maps.ℑ"></a><a id="19410" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#19410" class="Function">ℑ</a> <a id="19412" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="19414" href="Algebras.Products.html#2276" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="19417" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#19349" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="19419" href="Universes.html#403" class="Function Operator">̇</a>
 <a id="19422" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#19410" class="Function">ℑ</a> <a id="19424" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="19426" href="MGS-MLTT.html#3074" class="Function">Σ</a> <a id="19428" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#19428" class="Bound">𝑨</a> <a id="19430" href="MGS-MLTT.html#3074" class="Function">꞉</a> <a id="19432" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="19433" href="Algebras.Algebras.html#674" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="19441" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#19349" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="19443" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#525" class="Bound">𝑆</a><a id="19444" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="19446" href="MGS-MLTT.html#3074" class="Function">,</a> <a id="19448" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="19449" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#19428" class="Bound">𝑨</a> <a id="19451" href="Relations.Discrete.html#2494" class="Function Operator">∈</a> <a id="19453" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#2875" class="Datatype">S</a><a id="19454" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="19455" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#19349" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="19456" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="19458" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#19349" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="19459" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="19461" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#19372" class="Bound">𝒦</a><a id="19462" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="19464" href="MGS-MLTT.html#3515" class="Function Operator">×</a> <a id="19466" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="19467" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#19363" class="Bound">X</a> <a id="19469" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="19471" href="Overture.Preliminaries.html#12413" class="Function Operator">∣</a> <a id="19473" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#19428" class="Bound">𝑨</a> <a id="19475" href="Overture.Preliminaries.html#12413" class="Function Operator">∣</a><a id="19476" class="Symbol">)</a>

</pre>
Notice that the second component of this dependent pair type is  `(𝑨 ∈ 𝒦) × (X → ∣ 𝑨 ∣)`. In previous versions of the [UALib][] this second component was simply `𝑨 ∈ 𝒦`, until we realized that adding the type `X → ∣ 𝑨 ∣` is quite useful. Later we will see exactly why, but for now suffice it to say that a map of type `X → ∣ 𝑨 ∣` may be viewed abstractly as an *ambient context*, or more concretely, as an assignment of *values* in `∣ 𝑨 ∣` to *variable symbols* in `X`.  When computing with or reasoning about products, while we don't want to rigidly impose a context in advance, want do want to lay our hands on whatever context is ultimately assumed.  Including the "context map" inside the index type `ℑ` of the product turns out to be a convenient way to achieve this flexibility.


Taking the product over the index type ℑ requires a function that maps an index `i : ℑ` to the corresponding algebra.  Each `i : ℑ` is a triple, say, `(𝑨 , p , h)`, where `𝑨 : Algebra 𝓤 𝑆`, `p : 𝑨 ∈ 𝒦`, and `h : X → ∣ 𝑨 ∣`, so the function mapping an index to the corresponding algebra is simply the first projection.

<pre class="Agda">

 <a id="class-products-with-maps.𝔄"></a><a id="20611" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#20611" class="Function">𝔄</a> <a id="20613" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="20615" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#19410" class="Function">ℑ</a> <a id="20617" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="20619" href="Algebras.Algebras.html#674" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="20627" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#19349" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="20629" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#525" class="Bound">𝑆</a>
 <a id="20632" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#20611" class="Function">𝔄</a> <a id="20634" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="20636" class="Symbol">λ</a> <a id="20638" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="20639" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#20639" class="Bound">i</a> <a id="20641" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="20643" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#19410" class="Function">ℑ</a><a id="20644" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="20646" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="20648" href="Overture.Preliminaries.html#12413" class="Function Operator">∣</a> <a id="20650" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#20639" class="Bound">i</a> <a id="20652" href="Overture.Preliminaries.html#12413" class="Function Operator">∣</a>

</pre>

Finally, we define `class-product` which represents the product of all members of 𝒦.

<pre class="Agda">

 <a id="class-products-with-maps.class-product"></a><a id="20768" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#20768" class="Function">class-product</a> <a id="20782" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="20784" href="Algebras.Algebras.html#674" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="20792" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="20793" href="Algebras.Products.html#2276" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="20796" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#19349" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="20797" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="20799" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#525" class="Bound">𝑆</a>
 <a id="20802" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#20768" class="Function">class-product</a> <a id="20816" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="20818" href="Algebras.Products.html#1173" class="Function">⨅</a> <a id="20820" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#20611" class="Function">𝔄</a>

</pre>

If `p : 𝑨 ∈ 𝒦` and `h : X → ∣ 𝑨 ∣`, we view the triple `(𝑨 , p , h) ∈ ℑ` as an index over the class, and so we can think of `𝔄 (𝑨 , p , h)` (which is simply `𝑨`) as the projection of the product `⨅ 𝔄` onto the `(𝑨 , p, h)`-th component.



<pre class="Agda">

 <a id="class-products-with-maps.class-prod-s-∈-ps"></a><a id="21090" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#21090" class="Function">class-prod-s-∈-ps</a> <a id="21108" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="21110" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#20768" class="Function">class-product</a> <a id="21124" href="Relations.Discrete.html#2494" class="Function Operator">∈</a> <a id="21126" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#3564" class="Datatype">P</a><a id="21127" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="21128" href="Algebras.Products.html#2276" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="21131" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#19349" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="21132" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="21134" href="Algebras.Products.html#2276" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="21137" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#19349" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="21138" class="Symbol">}(</a><a id="21140" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#2875" class="Datatype">S</a> <a id="21142" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#19372" class="Bound">𝒦</a><a id="21143" class="Symbol">)</a>

  <a id="21192" class="Keyword">where</a>
  <a id="21200" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#21200" class="Function">lA</a> <a id="21203" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#21203" class="Function">llA</a> <a id="21207" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="21209" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#19410" class="Function">ℑ</a> <a id="21211" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="21213" href="Algebras.Algebras.html#674" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="21221" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="21222" href="Algebras.Products.html#2276" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="21225" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#19349" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="21226" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="21228" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#525" class="Bound">𝑆</a>

  <a id="21264" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#21203" class="Function">llA</a> <a id="21268" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#21268" class="Bound">i</a> <a id="21270" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="21272" href="Algebras.Algebras.html#4650" class="Function">lift-alg</a> <a id="21281" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="21282" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#21200" class="Function">lA</a> <a id="21285" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#21268" class="Bound">i</a><a id="21286" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="21288" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="21289" href="Algebras.Products.html#2276" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="21292" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#19349" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="21293" class="Symbol">)</a>

  <a id="21298" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#21298" class="Function">slA</a> <a id="21302" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="21304" class="Symbol">∀</a> <a id="21306" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#21306" class="Bound">i</a> <a id="21308" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="21310" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="21311" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#21200" class="Function">lA</a> <a id="21314" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#21306" class="Bound">i</a><a id="21315" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="21317" href="Relations.Discrete.html#2494" class="Function Operator">∈</a> <a id="21319" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#2875" class="Datatype">S</a> <a id="21321" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#19372" class="Bound">𝒦</a>
