  <a id="21425" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#21425" class="Function">psPllA</a> <a id="21432" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="21434" href="Algebras.Products.html#1173" class="Function">⨅</a> <a id="21436" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#21203" class="Function">llA</a> <a id="21440" href="Relations.Discrete.html#2494" class="Function Operator">∈</a> <a id="21442" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#3564" class="Datatype">P</a> <a id="21444" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="21445" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#2875" class="Datatype">S</a> <a id="21447" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#19372" class="Bound">𝒦</a><a id="21448" class="Symbol">)</a>
  <a id="21452" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#21425" class="Function">psPllA</a> <a id="21459" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="21461" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#3854" class="InductiveConstructor">produ</a> <a id="21467" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#21364" class="Function">psllA</a>

  <a id="21476" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#21476" class="Function">llA≅A</a> <a id="21482" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="21484" class="Symbol">∀</a> <a id="21486" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#21486" class="Bound">i</a> <a id="21488" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="21490" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="21491" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#21203" class="Function">llA</a> <a id="21495" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#21486" class="Bound">i</a><a id="21496" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="21498" href="Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#1049" class="Function Operator">≅</a> <a id="21500" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="21501" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#20611" class="Function">𝔄</a> <a id="21503" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#21486" class="Bound">i</a><a id="21504" class="Symbol">)</a>
  <a id="21508" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#21476" class="Function">llA≅A</a> <a id="21514" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#21514" class="Bound">i</a> <a id="21516" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="21518" href="Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#1826" class="Function">≅-trans</a> <a id="21526" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="21527" href="Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#1648" class="Function">≅-sym</a> <a id="21533" href="Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#2841" class="Function">lift-alg-≅</a><a id="21543" class="Symbol">)(</a><a id="21545" href="Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#1648" class="Function">≅-sym</a> <a id="21551" href="Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#2841" class="Function">lift-alg-≅</a><a id="21561" class="Symbol">)</a>

</pre>

So, since `PS⊆SP`, we see that that the product of all subalgebras of a class `𝒦` belongs to `SP(𝒦)`.

<pre class="Agda">

 <a id="class-products-with-maps.class-prod-s-∈-sp"></a><a id="21694" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#21694" class="Function">class-prod-s-∈-sp</a> <a id="21712" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="21714" href="MGS-FunExt-from-Univalence.html#2235" class="Function">hfunext</a> <a id="21722" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="21723" href="Algebras.Products.html#2276" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="21726" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#19349" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="21727" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="21729" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="21730" href="Algebras.Products.html#2276" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="21733" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#19349" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="21734" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="21736" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="21738" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#20768" class="Function">class-product</a> <a id="21752" href="Relations.Discrete.html#2494" class="Function Operator">∈</a> <a id="21754" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#2875" class="Datatype">S</a><a id="21755" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="21756" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#3564" class="Datatype">P</a> <a id="21758" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#19372" class="Bound">𝒦</a><a id="21759" class="Symbol">)</a>
 <a id="21762" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#21694" class="Function">class-prod-s-∈-sp</a> <a id="21780" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#21780" class="Bound">hfe</a> <a id="21784" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="21786" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#15554" class="Function">PS⊆SP</a> <a id="21792" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#21780" class="Bound">hfe</a> <a id="21796" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#21090" class="Function">class-prod-s-∈-ps</a>

</pre>
